## ğŸ¤” What is Nano Banana Pro?

**Nano Banana Pro** is Google's latest multimodal AI model featuring:

- ğŸ¯ **Multimodal Understanding** - Process text, images, and video
- ğŸ¨ **High-Quality Generation** - Photorealistic to artistic styles
- âš¡ **Fast Iteration** - Quick edits and variations
- ğŸŒˆ **Diverse Styles** - From pixel art to oil paintings
- ğŸ”§ **Precise Control** - Detailed composition and lighting
- ğŸ“ **Complex Scenes** - Multi-object, multi-character rendering

ğŸ“š **Learn More:** [Nano Banana Pro: 10 Real Cases](https://youmind.com/blog/nano-banana-pro-10-real-cases)

### ğŸš€ Raycast Integration

Some prompts support **dynamic arguments** using [Raycast Snippets](https://raycast.com/help/snippets) syntax. Look for the ğŸš€ Raycast Friendly badge!

**Example:**
```
A quote card with "{argument name="quote" default="Stay hungry, stay foolish"}"
by {argument name="author" default="Steve Jobs"}
```

When used in Raycast, you can dynamically replace the arguments for quick iterations!

### No. 6: Luxury minimalist product photography based on a reference image

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A prompt for generating high-end, minimalist commercial product photography in the style of luxury brand ads, using an uploaded reference image of the core product as the base.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Using my uploaded reference image as the base, generate a minimalist, high-quality commercial still life photograph with the aesthetic of a luxury brand advertisement.

Preserve the general shape, proportions, and main color scheme of the core product in the reference so that it is instantly recognizable as the same product, but upgrade the overall texture and atmosphere of the image, making it look like an ad for a top-tier international fragrance, skincare item, or high-end electronic product.

Use a vertical 4:5 composition. The background should be a large area of clean, neutral negative space, such as soft off-white, cool gray, or light beige, creating a quiet, restrained, and expensive studio environment. Apart from the core product and a minimal number of necessary supports, do not add any extra decorations. No clutter, no elaborate scene setupâ€”only keep very simple geometric supports (such as a plain white cube, a cylinder, or a thin transparent panel). The supports must be simple and low-profile, existing only to hold and accentuate the product.

Strongly emphasize the material details of the product, and let the lighting fully serve those materials:
Show frosted glass with a fine, soft matte texture, ceramics with a matte or slightly glazed feel, and polished metal with clean, sharp specular highlights. Liquids should have clearly visible viscosity and volume. Avoid any cheap plastic feel, complex patterns, or gaudy stickers; the overall material quality must feel cool, restrained, and luxurious.

Use professional studio lighting: mainly soft, diffused light from softboxes, plus precise rim light outlining the productâ€™s shape. The contours should be crisp and layered, and the shadows should be soft and clean, with no noise or dirty shadow patches. You may use a near-macro viewpoint, moving in closer to the product to highlight materials and details, while preserving ample negative space around the frame so the product can "speak for itself" in the emptiness.

Keep the overall color scheme neutral and calm. The productâ€™s own color can be slightly more saturated, making it the single visual focal point in the scene. Do not use exaggerated gradient backgrounds, flashy colored lighting, or e-commerce promo aesthetics. No large-price text, labels, or cartoon graphics.

The final result must be a high-resolution commercial key visual that looks ready for a magazine back cover or a high-end brand announcement poster: minimalist, quiet, high-end, with the core product confidently centered, surrounded by clean negative space and precisely controlled lighting.
```

#### ğŸ–¼ï¸ Generated Images

##### Image 1

<div align="center">
<img src="https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1764915823213_skhwpb_G7Qvxi5bIAAqpfX.jpg" width="700" alt="Luxury minimalist product photography based on a reference image - Image 1">
</div>

#### ğŸ“Œ Details

- **Author:** [VoxcatAI](https://x.com/VoxcatAI)
- **Source:** [Twitter Post](https://x.com/VoxcatAI/status/1996273073725780161)
- **Published:** December 3, 2025
- **Languages:** zh

### No. 7: London outdoor restaurant portrait with Nano Banana Pro

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A photorealistic prompt for a young woman at a calm London outdoor restaurant on a crisp March morning, with shallow depth of field and candid phone-photo vibes.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Create a photorealistic image of a young woman sitting at a relaxed outdoor restaurant in {argument name="city in english" default="London"} on a cool Wednesday morning in March {argument name="year in english" default="2025"}. The sky is clear, the spring air is crisp, and the city feels calm as it wakes up. She is the focal point of the shotâ€”wearing a light scarf, gently stirring her tea while gazing off to the side with a thoughtful expression. Everything behind her, from the waiter moving about to the soft morning traffic, should fall into a smooth blur, giving the picture the effortless, candid atmosphere of a moment casually snapped on a phone.
```

#### ğŸ–¼ï¸ Generated Images

##### Image 1

<div align="center">
<img src="https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1764909307226_bcwb2i_G7QIraQaoAANflM.jpg" width="700" alt="London outdoor restaurant portrait with Nano Banana Pro - Image 1">
</div>

### No. 9: Detailed mirror-selfie otaku room scene

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A very detailed Nano Banana prompt describing a female mirror selfie in a blue-toned otaku computer corner, with full specifications for character, environment, lighting, camera, and negative prompts.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
### Scene
Mirror selfie in an otaku-style computer corner, blue color tone.

### Subject
* Gender expression: female
* Age: around 25
* Ethnicity: East Asian
* Body type: slim, with a defined waist; natural body proportions
* Skin tone: light neutral tone
* Hairstyle:
    * Length: waist-length hair
    * Style: straight with slightly curled ends
    * Color: medium brown
* Pose:
    * Stance: standing in a slight contrapposto pose
    * Right hand: holding a smartphone in front of her face (identity hidden)
    * Left arm: naturally hanging down alongside the torso
    * Torso: body leaning slightly back; waist and abdomen exposed
* Clothing:
    * Top: light blue cropped knit cardigan, top two buttons fastened; a blue French-style bra faintly visible
    * Bottom: denim ultra-short shorts, with a blue satin ribbon bow on each side of the hips
    * Socks: blue and white horizontal striped over-the-knee socks
    * Accessory: a blue cute mascot phone case

### Environment
* Description: bedroom computer corner seen through a wall-mounted mirror
* Furnishings:
    * White desk
    * Single monitor showing a soft blue wallpaper (no readable text)
    * Mechanical keyboard with white keycaps on a blue desk mat
    * Mouse on a small blue mouse pad
    * PC tower on the right side with blue case lighting
    * Three anime figures on or near the PC tower
    * A poster of a pagoda on the wall
    * Cat-shaped desk lamp with blue accents
    * A transparent glass of water
    * A tall green leafy plant by the window (on the left side of the frame)
* Color replacement: replace all originally pink elements (clothes and room decor) with blue tones (baby blue to sky blue/periwinkle blue).

### Lighting
* Light source: daylight coming from a large window on the left side of the camera, through sheer curtains
* Light quality: soft, diffused light
* White balance (K): 5200

### Camera
* Mode: smartphone rear camera shooting via the mirror (no portrait/bokeh mode)
* Equivalent focal length (mm): 26
* Distances (m):
    * Subject to mirror: 0.6
    * Camera to mirror: 0.5
* Exposure:
    * Aperture (f): 1.8
    * ISO: 100
    * Shutter speed (s): 0.01
    * Exposure compensation (EV): -0.3
* Focus: focus on the torso and shorts in the mirror image
* Depth of field: natural smartphone deep depth of field; background clearly visible with no artificial blur
* Composition:
    * Aspect ratio: 1:1
    * Crop: from the top of the head to mid-thigh; include the desk, monitor, PC tower, and plant in the frame
    * Angle: slightly high angle from the mirrorâ€™s point of view
    * Composition note: keep the subject centered; to avoid wide-angle edge distortion, have her stand a bit further away and crop to a square later.

### Negative prompts
* Any appearance of pink/magenta anywhere
* Beauty filters/over-smoothed skin; poreless skin look
* Exaggerated or distorted anatomy
* NSFW, see-through fabrics, wardrobe malfunctions
* Logos, brand names, or readable user interface text
* Fake portrait-mode blur, CGI/illustration feel
```

### No. 10: Edo-period Ukiyo-e reinterpretation of a modern scene

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly-structured image prompt to depict a modern-day scene reimagined as an Edo-period Japanese Ukiyo-e woodblock print, with detailed guidance on anachronistic tech, composition, texture, and color.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A Japanese Edo-period Ukiyo-e woodblock print. The overall feeling is a surreal collaboration between masters like Hokusai and Hiroshige, reimagining modern technology through an ancient lens.

**The scene:** {argument name="modern scene" default="a busy Shibuya scramble crossing"}

**Edo transformation logic:**
Characters wear Edo-era kimono but perform modern actions. All technology is transformed into surreal Edo equivalents:
* Smartphones are glowing, illustrated paper scrolls being read intently.
* Metro stations and trains are giant articulated wooden centipede carriages shuffling through crowds.
* Skyscrapers are reimagined as endless, towering wooden pagodas reaching into dramatic clouds.
* Robots and mecha appear as giant, armored woodblock golems.

The composition uses a flattened perspective with large, bold, hand-carved ink outlines. The background features heavily stylized Ukiyo-e wave patterns and dramatic, swirling clouds, with a distant Mt. Fuji visible on the horizon.

The image must look like a physical print, not a digital painting.
* Texture: strong visible wood grain texture and rough paper fibers throughout the piece.
* Printing imperfections: pigment bleeding is evident. Simulate hand-pressed plates with slight color misalignment for authenticity.
* Color palette: strictly limited to traditional mineral pigments, with dominant use of Prussian blue, vermilion red, and muted yellow ochre.
* Lighting: soft, flat, shadow-free lighting with no digital gradients.

Aspect ratio is 3:4 vertical poster. Include vertical Japanese calligraphy describing the scene and a traditional red artist seal stamp in a corner.
```

### No. 5: Profile / Avatar - Identity-Locked Mirror Selfie Pose Recreation Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly technical, structured prompt for Gemini Nano Banana Pro 3.0, designed to recreate a specific mirror selfie pose while strictly locking all scene parameters (camera angle, distance, mirror geometry, clothing geometry, and pose) and only allowing the replacement of the subject's identity, ensuring ultra-realistic consistency across generations.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "template_id": "mirror_side_pose_workout_shorts_ultralock_v1_compact",
  "version": "1.0.1",

    "replace_identity_only": true,
    "preserve_body_proportions": true,

      20,
      35

  },

      "pitch_down": -2
    },

      ]
    }
  },
  "phone_lock": {
    "hand": "right",
    "position_xy": [
      0.38,
      0.47
    ],
    "orientation_degrees": {
      "yaw": 2
    },
    "grip": "fingers_wrapped_thumb_along_edge"

      "pelvis_yaw_deg": 80,
      "torso_yaw_deg": 65,
      "head_yaw_deg": 55
    },
    "spine": {
      "lumbar_curve": "soft",
      "thoracic_curve": "upright"
    },

        "side": "left",

          0.38,
          0.47
        ]
      },

      }

        0.8,

      ]
    },

      "chin_down_deg": 6,

    }

### No. 9: Profile / Avatar - E-Girl Mirror Selfie with Deep Depth of Field

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly technical JSON prompt for generating an 'E-Girl Mirror Selfie' with a minimalist goth style. It specifies engine configuration, including LoRA slots and sampling settings, but its core instruction is to enforce a deep depth of field (f/11) so that the subject, bed texture, and background wall are all sharp, contrasting the typical shallow depth of field in portraits.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "meta": {
    "project": "Egirl_FrogPose_PinkHK_Flux_V4.2",
    "target_engine": "Flux.1 [dev] / Nano Banana Pro",
    "version": "4.2.0 (Everything in Focus - f/11)",
    "created_at": "2025-12-18T20:55:00Z"
  },
  "engine_configuration": {
    "model": {
      "base": "flux1-dev.safetensors",
      "quantization": "fp8 / nf4",
      "vae": "ae.safetensors"
    },
    "lora_slots": [
      {
        "name": "Realism_LoRA_v2 (Optional)",
        "strength": 0.5,
        "note": "Enhances porcelain skin tone and fabric textures."
      }
    ],
    "sampling": {
      "sampler_name": "euler",
      "scheduler": "simple",
      "steps": 28,
      "guidance_scale": 2.5,
      "shift": 1.0
    },
    "dimensions": {
      "width": 1024,
      "height": 1536,
      "aspect_ratio": "2:3",
      "megapixel_class": "1.5MP"
    }
  },
  "prompt_construction": {
    "narrative_layer": {
      "style": "E-Girl Mirror Selfie / Minimalist Goth",
      "instruction": "Capture a sharp, full-body mirror selfie of a young woman sitting in a frog pose on a bed, focusing on the midriff and the pink phone case.",
      "subject_flow": "A pale 19-21 year old woman with black wolf-cut hair sitting on a grey bed with knees up, holding a pink Hello Kitty phone."
    },
    "texture_layer": {
      "skin_physics": "pale porcelain skin, smooth texture, rosy blush, glossy lips, e-girl eyeliner",
      "fabric_physics": "ribbed knit texture of black tube top, metal grommets on belt, cotton texture of white socks, quilted grey duvet",
      "environment_physics": "SHARP DETAILS ON BACKGROUND: glass mirror reflection, white wall texture, window glass, grey fabric folds"
    },
    "camera_physics": {
      "lens_imperfections": "smartphone camera aesthetic, high fidelity",
      "focus": "DEEP DEPTH OF FIELD (f/11) - NO BLUR. The woman, the bed texture, and the background wall are all sharp.",
      "settings": "Smartphone Simulation, 24mm Lens, 1/60s, ISO 300 (Diffused Window Light)"
    },
    "color_grading": {
      "white_balance": "Cool Natural (Diffused Window Light)",
      "shadows": "Soft shadows defining the midriff",
      "highlights": "Soft highlights on skin and glossy phone case"
    }
  },
  "final_prompt_string": "A candid raw mirror selfie photograph shot on Smartphone f/11. Deep depth of field, everything in focus. A very slim 19-21 year old woman with pale porcelain skin and black hair with bangs (wolf cut) sitting on a dark grey bed in a 'frog pose' (knees bent, high and wide apart). She leans back slightly. She wears a black ribbed strapless tube top exposing her toned midriff, a low-rise black mini skirt with a heavy silver grommet belt, and white ankle socks with red Hello Kitty embroidery. She holds a phone with a light pink 3D Hello Kitty case. Dramatic e-girl eyeliner and glossy lips. Background is sharp and detailed: messy grey duvet and a plain white wall are clearly visible with no bokeh. "
```

### No. 11: Profile / Avatar - Ultra-Photorealistic Saree Mirror Selfie Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly structured JSON prompt for Gemini Nano Banana Pro, originally built on a ChatGPT prompt, designed for ultra-photorealistic image generation. It focuses on generating a mirror selfie of a young woman in a black saree and modern blouse, strictly preserving her facial and body identity from a reference image, and aiming for an editorial yet natural look with realistic fabric physics and skin texture.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "type": "{argument name="type" default="image_generation"}",
  "model_style": "{argument name="model style" default="ultra_photorealistic"}",

  "resolution": "{argument name="resolution" default="8K"}",
  "quality": "{argument name="quality" default="high_detail_realism"}",
  "identity_reference": {
    "use_reference_image": true,
    "face_preservation": "{argument name="face preservation" default="exact"}",
    "body_preservation": "{argument name="body preservation" default="exact"}",
    "no_facial_changes": true,
    "no_body_modification": true
  },
  "subject": {
    "gender": "{argument name="gender" default="female"}",
    "age": "{argument name="age" default="young adult"}",
    "expression": "{argument name="expression" default="soft confident gaze, natural lips slightly parted"}",
    "pose": "{argument name="pose" default="slightly angled mirror selfie pose, relaxed shoulders, natural posture"}",
    "hair": {
      "color": "{argument name="hair color" default="dark brown"}",
      "style": "{argument name="hair style" default="loose, natural volume, middle part"}",
      "texture": "{argument name="hair texture" default="smooth and realistic"}"
    },
    "skin": {
      "tone": "{argument name="skin tone" default="warm natural complexion"}",
      "detail": "{argument name="skin detail" default="visible skin texture, realistic highlights, no plastic look"}"
    }
  },
  "outfit": {
    "style": "{argument name="outfit style" default="black saree with modern blouse"}",
    "blouse": "{argument name="blouse" default="black sleeveless blouse with subtle shimmer embroidery"}",
    "saree": "{argument name="saree" default="black draped saree with soft fabric folds and realistic fabric physics"}",
    "accessories": [
      "{argument name="accessory 1" default="delicate waist chain"}",
      "{argument name="accessory 2" default="minimal jewelry"}"
    ]
  },
  "environment": {
    "location": "{argument name="location" default="indoor modern bedroom or dressing area"}",
    "background": "{argument name="background" default="clean white wardrobe cabinets"}",
    "lighting": {
      "type": "{argument name="lighting type" default="soft indoor lighting"}",
      "source": "{argument name="lighting source" default="overhead ceiling light"}",
      "effect": "{argument name="lighting effect" default="natural shadows, balanced highlights"}"
    }
  },
  "camera": {
    "device": "{argument name="device" default="smartphone"}",
    "lens": "{argument name="lens" default="natural portrait lens"}",
    "angle": "{argument name="angle" default="slightly above eye level"}",
    "focus": "{argument name="focus" default="sharp focus on subject, mild background softness"}",
    "depth_of_field": "{argument name="depth of field" default="realistic"}"
  },
  "rendering_rules": {
    "no_cartoon": true,
    "no_ai_artifacts": true,
    "no_over_smoothing": true,
    "no_extra_limbs": true,

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed JSON prompt designed for Nano Banana Pro to transform an input photo into a high-definition, warm-toned vintage portrait. "strict": true,

"The face MUST remain IDENTICAL to the input photo.",

]
},

"keep_texture": true,
"no_smoothing": true,
"no_blur": true,
"realistic_details": "natural texture preserved.",

"contrast":"+22",
"highlights":"-5",

]
},

"composition":{

"skin":"Natural undertone, realistic texture, NOT smoothed.",

"fabric_behavior":"Flash creates bright reflections and visible folds."
}

"id":"mirror",

"lighting":"Flash reflection visible but subdued."

"id":"flowers",

"id":"wall",
"description":"White paneled wall with framed signage."
}
],

"rules":{
"identity_constant": true,
"no_face_change": true,

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly specific image generation prompt for Gemini Nano Banana Pro, requiring strict adherence to a reference photo's facial identity. The prompt details a full-body mirror selfie pose (squatting low) in a romantic, fairy-core aesthetic, specifying the pastel pink corset dress, butterfly-adorned heels, and the charming floral cafe interior setting, aiming for 8K photorealism.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{

    "subject": {

      "facial_features": [
        "Preserve exact face shape",
        "Match eye structure and eyebrow shape",
        "Retain lip shape and natural color"
      ],
      "hair": "{argument name="hair color" default="black"}, exact hairstyle from reference",
      "makeup": "Natural style as per reference",
      "expression": "Soft, calm, looking at phone screen"
    },

    "apparel": {
      "main_garment": "Soft pastel {argument name="dress color" default="pink"}, romantic corset-style mini dress inspired by a fairy-core aesthetic. Long, sheer, flared sleeves that drape gracefully with light fabric transparency. Dress matches exactly the reference pink dress in color, silhouette, and romantic style.",
      "fabric_physics": "Lightweight chiffon and satin blend, airy movement, natural folds, soft wind-like flow",
      "footwear": "Pastel blush {argument name="shoe color" default="pink"} satin high-heeled sandals with a square toe. Delicate thin straps adorned with embroidered 3D butterfly appliquÃ©s across the front and ankle straps. Slim feminine heel, elegant fairy-core aesthetic, matching exactly the reference butterfly heels in color, texture, and romantic detail.",
      "accessories": [
        "Silver necklace",
        "Silver bracelet",
        "Silver rings"
      ]
    },

    "pose_and_action": {
      "type": "Full-body mirror selfie",
      "stance": "Squatting low gracefully, one knee forward, leaning slightly toward mirror",
      "head_position": "Tilted slightly downward",
      "hands": {
        "right_hand": "Holding phone vertically in front of face",
        "left_hand": "Resting gently on knee"
      },
      "props": "Smartphone with soft pink phone case, soft pastel tone, minimal design"
    },

    "environment": {
      "location": "Charming floral cafe interior",
      "background": "Romantic European-style floral cafe with stone-textured walls, hanging wicker baskets, dried flower arrangements, pastel floral bouquets, vintage wooden shelves, rustic beams, and soft decorative mirrors. Warm neutral stone tones mixed with soft pinks, greens, creams, and lavender florals. Cozy, aesthetic, feminine atmosphere.",
      "flooring": "Vintage patterned tile floor with subtle reflections"
    },

    "lighting_and_atmosphere": {
      "quality": "Soft, ambient cafe lighting with gentle highlights",
      "mood": "Feminine, romantic, elegant, fairy-core, social media aesthetic"
    },

    "technical_specifications": {

**Lighting:** Even, professional gallery lighting highlighting the coat's texture and the details of the background prints.

--ar 9:16 --v 6.0

A detailed image generation prompt designed for Google Gemini Nano Banana Pro, focusing on creating a photorealistic, high-definition fashion photograph.       "perspective": "Eye-level.",

    }
  },
  "generation_prompt": "A photorealistic full-body shot of a young woman with long {argument name="hair color" default="brown"} hair leaning against a {argument name="wall color" default="grey"} wall, wearing a short {argument name="dress color" default="white"} sleeveless mini dress with a flowy skirt. ### No. 30: Infographic / Edu Visual - Culinary Periodic Table Display Board Generator

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A complex instructional prompt designed to generate a visual representation of a dish's flavor profile in the style of a scientific periodic table. It requires analyzing a dish's ingredients and flavor compounds, then rendering a detailed display board with color-coded compartments, molecular structures, and a handwritten recipe, combining chemistry aesthetics with product design.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
<instruction> 
Input A is a famous dish (photo or dish name). Analyze the dish's complete ingredient breakdown, primary flavor compounds, chemical interactions, and scientific basis for why ingredients work together.
Optional Input B is a style reference (laboratory equipment / tech product packaging). If missing, choose scientific periodic table meets Apple product design aesthetic.
Goal: Grid-format display board (20"x16") in periodic table structure, with each ingredient in its own compartment labeled with both culinary and scientific information, color-coded by flavor profile.
Rules:

Brushed aluminum, white acrylic, or frosted glass backing
20-30 small clear compartments in periodic table grid layout
Each compartment contains: ingredient specimen, common name, scientific name, primary flavor molecule
Color-coded borders: umami (red), sweet (pink), sour (yellow), bitter (green), fat (orange), aromatic (purple)
Center "legend" section: 3D molecular structure diagram of signature compound
Lower corner: actual handwritten recipe on aged vellum or parchment under glass
AR markers for scanning to see animated 3D molecule models
Clean sans-serif typography (like Helvetica or Futura)
Minimal design with generous white space
Include atomic-style "numbers" for each ingredient showing ratio/importance

Output: ONE image, 4:5 clean product photography style with soft shadows on pure white background
</instruction>
```

### No. 44: YouTube Thumbnail - Photorealistic MacBook Screen POV Selfie Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A complex JSON prompt for Gemini Nano Banana Pro designed for image-to-image generation, focusing on creating an ultra-realistic POV shot looking down at a MacBook screen. The screen displays a Photo Booth live preview of the subject (whose identity is strictly preserved from the input photo) in a dim bedroom, with Spotify running in the background. The prompt emphasizes realism details like RGB pixel grids, dust, and natural noise, simulating a photo taken of a screen rather than a screenshot.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "image_settings": {
    "aspect_ratio": "3:4",
    "resolution": {
      "width": 1152,
      "height": 1536
    }
  },

  "prompt": {
    "identity_lock": {
      "reference": "{argument name="reference" default="input_photo"}",
      "preserve": [
        "{argument name="preserve 1" default="face"}",
        "{argument name="preserve 2" default="facial proportions"}",
        "{argument name="preserve 3" default="eye shape"}",
        "{argument name="preserve 4" default="nose"}",
        "{argument name="preserve 5" default="lips"}",
        "{argument name="preserve 6" default="skin tone"}",
        "{argument name="preserve 7" default="skin texture"}",
        "{argument name="preserve 8" default="hairline"}",
        "{argument name="preserve 9" default="overall identity"}"
      ],
      "rules": [
        "{argument name="rule 1" default="no face swap"}",
        "{argument name="rule 2" default="no beautify"}",
        "{argument name="rule 3" default="no smoothing"}",
        "{argument name="rule 4" default="no reshaping"}",
        "{argument name="rule 5" default="no AI look"}"
      ]
    },

    "scene": {
      "camera_angle": "{argument name="camera angle" default="high-angle downward shot, POV"}",
      "composition": "{argument name="composition" default="MacBook screen fills most of the frame, thin strip of physical keyboard visible at the bottom"}",
      "screen_surface": [
        "{argument name="screen surface 1" default="visible RGB pixel grid"}",
        "{argument name="screen surface 2" default="subtle moire effect"}",
        "{argument name="screen surface 3" default="micro dust on glass"}",
        "{argument name="screen surface 4" default="faint fingerprints"}",
        "{argument name="screen surface 5" default="soft ambient reflections"}"
      ]
    },

    "digital_interface": {
      "os": "{argument name="os" default="macOS dark mode"}",
      "background_app": {
        "name": "{argument name="background app name" default="Spotify"}",
        "view": "{argument name="background app view" default="Liked Songs"}",
        "visible_tracks": [
          "{argument name="track 1" default="Blank Space â€“ Taylor Swift"}",
          "{argument name="track 2" default="Shake It Off â€“ Taylor Swift"}",
          "{argument name="track 3" default="Cruel Summer â€“ Taylor Swift"}",
          "{argument name="track 4" default="Love Story â€“ Taylor Swift"}"
        ]
      },
      "foreground_app": {
        "name": "{argument name="foreground app name" default="Photo Booth"}",
        "state": "{argument name="foreground app state" default="live preview window"}",
        "position": "{argument name="foreground app position" default="floating, center-right"}"
      }
    },

    "photo_booth_content": {
      "environment": {
        "room": "{argument name="room" default="dim bedroom"}",
        "background": "{argument name="background" default="off-white wall, rumpled bedding"}",
        "lighting": "{argument name="lighting" default="low-light, nocturnal, cool screen glow mixed with warm skin tones"}"
      },
      "subject": {
        "pose": "{argument name="subject pose" default="lying down, relaxed, candid"}",
        "expression": "{argument name="subject expression" default="natural, slightly relaxed"}",
        "outfit": "{argument name="subject outfit" default="light-colored tank top"}",
        "prop": {
          "item": "{argument name="prop item" default="iPhone 15 Pro"}",
          "hand": "{argument name="prop hand" default="right hand"}"
        }
      }
    },

    "realism_rules": [
      "{argument name="realism rule 1" default="this is a photo of a screen, not a screenshot"}",
      "{argument name="realism rule 2" default="raw smartphone photo look"}",
      "{argument name="realism rule 3" default="natural noise"}",
      "{argument name="realism rule 4" default="imperfect glass"}",
      "{argument name="realism rule 5" default="no studio lighting"}",
      "{argument name="realism rule 6" default="no HD polish"}"
    ]
  },

  "negative_prompt": [
    "{argument name="negative 1" default="screenshot"}",
    "{argument name="negative 2" default="flat UI"}",
    "{argument name="negative 3" default="perfect screen"}",
    "{argument name="negative 4" default="clean glass"}",
    "{argument name="negative 5" default="studio lighting"}",
    "{argument name="negative 6" default="beauty filter"}",
    "{argument name="negative 7" default="cartoon"}",
    "{argument name="negative 8" default="3d render"}",
    "{argument name="negative 9" default="painting"}",
    "{argument name="negative 10" default="watermark"}",
    "{argument name="negative 11" default="blurred face"}"
  ]
}
```

### No. 47: YouTube Thumbnail - Character 'Participation Screen' Reveal Prompt

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly structured, multi-layered prompt for Nano Banana Pro designed to create a dramatic 'Participation Screen' or reveal splash image for a character based on a reference image. It strictly preserves the character's identity and style while placing them in a 16:9 composition with a headline text ('å‚æˆ¦!!' - 'Participate!!') and a simple, atmospheric background.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
layering:
  order:
    - text_layer
    - character_layer
    - background_layer
  strict: true

subject:
  description: >
    Preserve the subject exactly as in the reference image, keeping all facial features,
    colors, hairstyle, clothing, and proportions. No redesign or reinterpretation.
  framing: >
    Bust-up composition (head to upper torso), making the subject appear large and prominent.
  integrity: full_identity_preservation
  detail_level: ultra_high_resolution
  micro_details: preserve_skin_texture_hair_edges_fabric_details

composition:
  aspect_ratio: "16:9"
  layout: >
    Subject positioned on one side; headline text on the opposite side.
  emphasis: >
    Strong presence on the character's upper body and expression.

action:
  description: >
    Minimal motion enhancement. Maintain the reference pose while adding subtle dramatic energy.

location:
  description: >
    Simple background created by interpreting the reference imageâ€™s mood.
    Use soft gradients, atmospheric glow, light particles, or abstract light rays.
    Avoid complex textures or any copyrighted shapes.
    Background must NOT contain any characters, silhouettes, faces, bodies,
    or blurred forms derived from the subject.
  background_feel: >
    Subtle, atmospheric, clean.
  allowed_elements: pure_color_gradients_light_abstract_shapes_only
  prohibit_subject_reuse_in_background: true

style:
  visual_style: >
    High-impact reveal-splash aesthetic with strong contrast between character and headline.
  text_effects: >
    Metallic, high-energy lettering with pronounced depth and perspective. No glow effects.
  character_rendering: >
    Extremely high-resolution rendering with sharp facial details, clean hair definition,
    precise edges, and crisp texture fidelity.
  background_style_rules: >
    Background must be purely non-figurative. No silhouettes, no blurred shapes,
    and no reused subject elements.
  ink_splash_rules: >
    Ink splash must be pure black only. No other colors, tinting, blending, or variation.

camera_lighting:
  camera_angle: from_reference
  lighting: >
    Enhance with dramatic key lighting and subtle rim highlights to emphasize the reveal.
  clarity: maximum_definition

colors:
  palette: >
    Background colors inferred from the reference image.
    Character name in metallic silver; announcement text in saturated yellow.
  mood: dramatic, heroic, high_energy

text:
  character_name: "{argument name="character name" default="ã‚­ãƒ£ãƒ©ã‚¯ã‚¿ãƒ¼å"}"
  announcement_fixed: "Participate!!"
  placement: opposite_side_of_character
  p
```

### No. 48: YouTube Thumbnail - Cognitive Science-Based High-CTR Thumbnail Design Prompt

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A sophisticated system prompt designed for Nano Banana Pro to create high Click-Through Rate (CTR) thumbnails based on principles of cognitive science (neuroscience, psychology, behavioral economics). It instructs the AI to adopt the persona of an expert art director, analyze input text, and follow a detailed thinking process (Thinking Mode) before drawing, focusing on facial activation, pop-out effects, and minimizing cognitive load. It includes specific design and typography instructions.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
You are an expert in the "Adaptive Salience Model," creatively integrating knowledge from cognitive science (neuroscience, psychology, behavioral economics), and you are a top-tier art director.

Deeply analyze the [Input Text (Article Title or Beginning)] provided at the end, and generate a thumbnail image that maximizes the CTR (Click-Through Rate) for that article.

If a reference image is attached, place that character as the "person presenting the article content" and maintain consistency.

â–¼ Instructions for Generation Process (Thinking Process)
Use Nano Banana Pro's "Thinking Mode" to logically formulate the composition plan in the following steps before drawing:

1.  **[Step 1: Content Analysis and Hook Extraction]**
    * Identify the "maximum benefit the reader gains" or the "risk of loss if they don't know" from the input text (Application of Prospect Theory).
    * Select the most intuitive visual metaphor symbolizing the article's theme (e.g., rise, key, lightning, light, darkness, etc.).

2.  **[Step 2: Optimization by Adaptive Salience Model]**
    * **FFA Activation (Face Fusiform Area)**: Maximize the resolution of the character's face, especially the "eyes," and design the composition so that the gaze meets the viewer's (eye contact). Match the expression to the article's tone (surprise, confidence, seriousness, etc.).
    * **Pop-out Effect**: Use "vivid colors (neon colors or yellow, etc.)" that are complementary to the background color for the title text and important icons to create visual prominence.
    * **Cognitive Load Theory**: Do not overload the information. Limit elements to "1 face + 1 impactful text + 1 background metaphor."

3.  **[Step 3: Layout Design]**
    * Design the layout, considering the Z-pattern or F-pattern, so that the viewer's gaze flows from the "face" â†’ "high jump-rate text" â†’ "clickable element."

â–¼ Design and Style Specification
* **Composition**: Close-up (bust shot) or medium shot. Place the character in the center or at the intersection of the rule of thirds.
* **Taste/Aesthetic**: [Optimize for the genre of the input text. Examples: For business, "sophisticated, trustworthy"; for entertainment, "vibrant, high saturation"; for technology, "cyberpunk, futuristic"]
* **Text Rendering (Important)**:
    * Extract the **most catchy short phrase (recommended 10 characters or less)** from the input text.
    * **Font**: Use "**Heavy Serif**" font. To enhance readability, the text must have a **thick outline** contrasting with the background color.
    * **Placement (Jump Rate)**: **Set a high "Jump Rate."** Place the main keywords extremely large, and auxiliary words or sub-information small, creating visual rhythm and contrast.
* **Character Direction**: If there is a reference character, adjust their attire to match the article's theme (lab coat, suit, explorer, casual, etc.).

â–¼ Input Text
{argument name="input text" default="(Article title or content)"}
```

### No. 49: YouTube Thumbnail - Advanced Two-Step Prompting Strategy for Nano Banana Pro Thumbnails

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

This tweet outlines an advanced, two-step prompting strategy to significantly improve the quality of AI output, specifically for generating YouTube thumbnails using Nano Banana Pro. The strategy involves first asking a powerful LLM (like GPT-5.2) to systematically summarize the best practices, terminology, and constraints for creating Nano Banana Pro prompts (creating a 'map'). Then, the user asks the LLM to generate the final, specific prompt based on that established system and the user's requirements, resulting in much more consistent and targeted output.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Actually, there's a trickier way to use this.

First, have it systematically summarize the information
â†’ Then, based on that, have it create the output/deepen the discussion
Just doing this makes the quality of the output completely different.

This is because if you first create a blueprint in the AI's mindâ€”including "terminology," "judgment criteria," "prohibited items," "patterns," and "priorities"â€”

The next instructions will be output according to that blueprint, making it less likely to deviate.

For example, if you want Nano Banana Pro to create a thumbnail:

â‘  First, ask GPT-5.2:
"Thoroughly research and systematize the best practices for creating prompts for YouTube thumbnails using Nano Banana Pro. Include common mistakes as well."

â‘¡ After that, ask:
"Based on the current system, create a prompt for making a YouTube thumbnail on the theme of {argument name="theme" default="XX"} using Nano Banana Pro. The video content is like this, and I want to include {argument name="wording" default="this kind of wording"}."

Then, input the completed prompt into Nano Banana Pro. It becomes much easier to get the desired output.

If you just ask it to "create" every time, the AI outputs based on the moment, leading to inconsistent results. But if you create a map (system) first, it's powerful.

Moreover, this method works for side business strategies, sales copy, and video scripts. The versatility is insane.

I highly recommend having the AI organize how to create good output before having it perform the task, and then having it think based on that organization.

By the way, the thumbnail created this time is the third image.
Since the first attempt was mediocre, I had it systematize how to create attractive YouTube thumbnails before generating the prompt.
```

### No. 54: YouTube Thumbnail - Nano Banana Pro Battle Entry Screen Prompt

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed prompt structure for Nano Banana Pro designed to generate a dramatic 'battle entry screen' for a character based on a reference image. It uses a specific layering and composition structure (16:9 aspect ratio) to create a high-impact visual reveal, similar to a mecha anime or fighting game aesthetic. The prompt is highly structured, defining subject preservation, framing, layout, style, lighting, and color palette.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
layering:
  order:
    - text_layer
    - character_layer
    - background_layer
  strict: true

subject:
  description: >
    Preserve the subject exactly as in the reference image, keeping all facial features,
    colors, hairstyle, clothing, and proportions. No redesign or reinterpretation.
  framing: >

  integrity: full_identity_preservation

composition:
  aspect_ratio: "16:9"
  layout: >

  description: >

location:
  description: >
    Generate a simple, abstract background inferred from the tone of the reference image.
    No specific elements required; allow the model to interpret color and atmosphere freely.
    Background must NOT contain any characters, silhouettes, faces, bodies,
    or blurred forms derived from the subject.
  background_feel: clean_and_minimal
  allowed_elements: pure_color_gradients_light_abstract_shapes_only
  prohibit_subject_reuse_in_background: true

style:
  visual_style: >
    High-impact reveal-splash aesthetic with strong contrast between character and headline.
  text_effects: >
    Metallic, high-energy lettering with pronounced depth and perspective. No glow effects.
  character_rendering: >
    Extremely high-resolution rendering with sharp facial details, clean hair definition,
    precise edges, and crisp texture fidelity.
  background_style_rules: >
    Background must be purely non-figurative. No silhouettes, no blurred shapes,
    and no reused subject elements.
  ink_splash_rules: >
    Ink splash must be pure black only. No other colors, tinting, blending, or variation.

camera_lighting:
  camera_angle: from_reference
  lighting: >
    Enhance with dramatic key lighting and subtle rim highlights to emphasize the reveal.
  clarity: maximum_definition

colors:
  palette: >
    Background colors inferred from the reference image.
    Character name in metallic silver; announcement text in saturated yellow.
  mood: dramatic, heroic, high_energy

text:
  character_name: "{argument name="character name" default="Character Name"}"
  announcement_fixed: "{argument name="announcement" default="Entering the Battle!!"}"
  placement: opposite_side_of_character
  perspective: >
    Pronounced perspective: front surface larger, back tapered with visible extrusion.
  character_name_style: >
    Metallic silver, b
```

### No. 62: Comic / Storyboard - Cinematic Contact Sheet Generation from Reference Image

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A complex, multi-step prompt designed to generate a cohesive 3x3 cinematic contact sheet based on an uploaded reference image. It instructs the model to internalize the scene and subject, then create a sequence of images captured from multiple distances and angles while maintaining absolute consistency in subject, location, lighting, and emotional tone.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Study the uploaded image carefully and fully internalize the scene: the subjectâ€™s appearance, clothing, posture, emotional state, and the surrounding environment. Treat this moment as a single frozen point in time.
Create a cinematic image set that feels like a photographer methodically explored this exact moment from multiple distances and angles, without changing anything about the subject or location.
All images must clearly belong to the same scene, captured under the same lighting conditions, weather, and atmosphere. Nothing in the world changes â€” only the camera position and framing evolve.
The emotional tone should remain consistent throughout the set, subtly expressed through posture, gaze, and micro-expressions rather than exaggerated acting.
Begin by observing the subject within the environment from afar, letting the surroundings dominate the frame and establish scale and mood.
Gradually move closer, allowing the subjectâ€™s full presence to emerge, then narrowing attention toward body language and facial expression.
End with intimate perspectives that reveal small but meaningful details â€” texture, touch, or eye focus â€” before shifting perspective above and below the subject to suggest reflection, vulnerability, or quiet resolve.
Across the sequence:
Wider views should emphasize space and atmosphere
Mid-range views should emphasize posture and emotional context
Close views should isolate feeling and detail
Perspective shifts (low and high angles) should feel purposeful and cinematic, not decorative
Depth of field must behave naturally: distant views remain mostly sharp, while closer frames introduce shallow focus and gentle background separation.
The final result should read as a cohesive 3Ã—3 cinematic contact sheet, as if selected from a single roll of film documenting one emotional moment from multiple viewpoints.
No text, symbols, signage, watermarks, numbers, or graphic elements may appear anywhere in the images.
Photorealistic rendering, cinematic color grading, and consistent visual realism are mandatory.
```

* **2K Clear Image**
* **Cartoon Illustration Texture:** Pen and ink sketch/hand-drawn lines, simple white space background

## Design Philosophy

* Tell stories using visual metaphors
* Simple but not simplistic, humorous but not shallow

* All pages maintain a unified style, color scheme, and texture

### No. 81: Product Marketing - High-End Conceptual Product Magazine Photography Prompt

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed, multi-section prompt for Nano Banana Pro designed to generate high-end, glossy magazine editorial photography of a unique, unexpected functional object conceptualized and designed by a specified brand. It includes strict requirements for concept invention, ultra-premium materials, cinematic studio lighting, and precise layout elements like logo and descriptive text placement.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{argument name="Brand Name" default="[Brand Name]"}: 
A high-end, glossy conceptual art magazine editorial photograph showcasing a unique, unexpected functional object conceptualized and designed by the brand.

**1. Concept and Object (AI Invention):** 
Based on the specified brand's design philosophy, heritage, and material vocabulary, the AI must invent a new type of practical product (not standard clothing, shoes, or bags). Examples may include home goods, tech accessories, tools, or sports equipment, reinterpreted through the brand's perspective. The object should feel sculptural yet functional.

**2. Materials and Details (Ultra High-End):** 
The object is made of high-end, highly tactile materials characteristic of the brand (e.g., oxidized exotic leather, brushed aerospace-grade titanium, sculptural matte ceramic, molded carbon fiber, or technical haute couture textiles). Every detail must be extremely realistic: visible stitching, microscopic material textures, precision engraving, and complex texture contrasts.

**3. Photography and Lighting (Cinematic Studio):** 
Shot with a medium format Phase One camera paired with a 100mm macro lens. Extremely shallow depth of field, with the main object sharply focused and the background blurred to a creamy smoothness. Lighting is exquisite studio softbox illumination: soft, enveloping fill light combined with precise contour light to highlight outlines and material textures.

**4. Environment:** 
Seamless, flawless, pure, ultra-light-toned studio cyclorama background (e.g., desaturated mint green, light pink, or yellowish-white), with no shadows.

**5. Layout and UI Elements (Strict Placement):** 
- **Bottom Right:** The brand's small, low-key, monochromatic gray logo. 
- **Bottom Left:** Small, extremely simple monochromatic gray text describing the invented product. Font style similar to Manrope Regular, with extremely tight tracking (kerning) and balanced line spacing. Example format: "CONCEPT STUDY: [AI inserts invented product name]. MATERIAL: [AI inserts primary material]. SS25."
```

person = {argument name="person" default="Woman"}

![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

 A detailed text prompt for Google Gemini Nano Banana Pro generating a photorealistic indoor lifestyle portrait of a young woman seated sideways on a rattan chair. The prompt specifies her pose (looking over her shoulder), attire (vintage 'FRISCO' graphic tee and denim cutoffs), environment (cozy bedroom), and technical details (50mm lens, shallow depth of field, natural skin texture), aiming for a casual, lived-in editorial aesthetic.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "prompt": "A photorealistic indoor lifestyle portrait of a young woman seated sideways on a woven rattan chair in a cozy, softly lit bedroom. She turns her upper body slightly and looks back over her shoulder toward the camera, creating a confident yet relaxed pose. She has straight, dark shoulder-length hair parted near the center, natural makeup with subtle contouring, and bold red lipstick. She wears a loose vintage-style cream graphic T-shirt with the word '{argument name="tshirt text" default="FRISCO"}' printed largely across the back with a retro illustration, paired with high-waisted light blue denim cutoff shorts with frayed hems, and clean white low-top sneakers. The room features hardwood floors, a bed with slightly rumpled white bedding in the background, pillows on the floor in the foreground, and casually scattered clothing for a lived-in feel. A partially visible wall poster adds character. Lighting is warm natural window light with soft shadows and gentle highlights. Shallow depth of field keeps the subject sharp while the background is softly blurred. Warm neutral color palette with beige, cream, denim blue, and natural wood tones. Full-frame camera look, medium focal length around 50mm, eye-level angle, lifestyle editorial photography style, high detail, realistic skin texture, natural proportions, no over-smoothing.",
  "negative_prompt": "{argument name="negative prompt" default="cartoon, anime, illustration, CGI, overprocessed, plastic skin, extreme blur, harsh lighting, oversaturated colors, distorted body proportions, extra limbs, low resolution, noise, watermark, logo, text artifacts"}",
  "style": "{argument name="style" default="photorealistic lifestyle editorial"}",
  "camera": {
    "focal_length_mm": {argument name="focal length" default="50"},
    "angle": "{argument name="angle" default="eye-level"}",
    "depth_of_field": "{argument name="depth of field" default="shallow"}"
  },
  "lighting": {
    "type": "{argument name="lighting type" default="natural window light"}",
    "quality": "{argument name="lighting quality" default="soft and warm"}"
  },
  "environment": "{argument name="environment" default="cozy indoor bedroom, casual lived-in aesthetic"}",
  "quality": {
    "detail_level": "{argument name="detail level" default="high"}",
    "realism": "{argument name="realism" default="photorealistic"}",
    "skin_texture": "{argument name="skin texture" default="natural"}"
  }
}
```

### No. 91: E-commerce Main Image - Streetwear Algorithm AI: Object-to-Wearable Conversion

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A complex, multi-step system prompt that instructs the AI to act as a 'Streetwear Algorithm' to convert any random input object into a corresponding 'Hypebeast' fashion item (Puffer Jacket, Sneaker, Backpack, or Sunglasses) based on the object's physical properties (Texture, Structure, Shape). The prompt then requires generating a studio product shot of the resulting wearable, ensuring it looks manufactured from the input object's parts/materials.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
<instruction>Act as the "Streetwear Algorithm" AI.</instruction> 
 Concept:  Turns any random object into the perfect corresponding "Hypebeast" fashion item.
 1. ANALYZE INPUT (Form & Physics): 
 Look at the attached image. Determine:
 Texture: ({argument name="texture options" default="Soft/Hard/Liquid/Glass"})
 Structure:  ({argument name="structure options" default="Rigid/Flexible/Mechanical"})
 Shape:  ({argument name="shape options" default="Boxy/Round/Aerodynamic/Flat"})
 2. AUTO-SELECT MODEL (Run this Logic Tree): 
 IF Input is Soft, Volumetric, or Tangled  (Noodles, Clouds, Moss, Bubblewrap)
 -> GENERATE: Oversized Puffer Jacket 
IF Input is Rigid, Aerodynamic, or Mechanical  (Stapler, Car, Power Tool, Robot)
 -> GENERATE: Chunky Conceptual Sneaker 
 IF Input is Boxy, Container-like, or Heavy Metal  (Safe, Trash Can, Speaker, Computer Case)
 -> GENERATE: Hard-Shell Tech Backpack 
 IF Input is Transparent, Glassy, or Thin/Wire-like  (Neon Sign, Circuit Board, Stained Glass, Ice)
 -> GENERATE: Futuristic Wrap-Around Sunglasses (Visor) 
 IF Input is Textile, Flat, or Pattern-Heavy** ({argument name="pattern input examples" default="Persian Rug, Painting, Cardboard"})
 -> GENERATE: Oversized Hoodie or Tactical Vest 
 
3. EXECUTE DESIGN: 
 Create a studio product shot of the "selected item".
 Design Rule:  The item must look like it was manufactured "using the parts/materials of the input object".
 Details:  Keep original branding/logos if present.
 Setting:  Floating pedestal, Cinematic Lighting, 8k Resolution.
```

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

Two highly specific, technical prompts designed to generate exploded-view diagrams of Apple products (Watch Ultra and iPhone) based on a reference image. The prompts focus on maintaining perspective, lighting, and spatial realism while separating components in a controlled, orderly sequence.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Apple Watch
Create a dynamic scene where the Apple Watch Ultra from Reference 1 breaks down into its individual components, with each piece leaving the dial in a controlled, forward-floating sequence that retains the original direction and perspective of the watch, maintaining the metallic finish, glass reflections, and rugged structure visible in the reference; place the detached orange strap behind the wrist while keeping the same soft, neutral studio lighting, the close-up composition of the arm, and the smooth muted background tone. Enhance micro-details, improve overall image fidelity, increase clarity, and make the colors more vibrant and saturated.

IPhone
Create a precise exploded-view animation of the Apple iPhone from Reference 1 where every internal and external layer, casing, glass, display, internal chips, modules, and structural parts, moves outward from the screen in a smooth, orderly chain, while keeping the same fixed viewpoint: a low frontal angle with the device vertical, right side slightly visible, left side largely hidden, the hand gripping the phone in the same position, and the soft diffused lighting unchanged; ensure each floating element is lit exactly like the main scene and casts subtle, accurate shadows onto adjacent parts and onto the hand, creating strong spatial realism without altering the composition. Enhance micro-details, improve overall image fidelity, increase clarity, and make the colors more vibrant and saturated.
```

iPhone

Lighting is dominated by a rear/side backlight, producing pronounced rim light around the hand and subtle edge highlights on the phoneâ€™s metal frame. The phoneâ€™s flat glass front has muted reflections, no glare, and the screen emits a smooth high-contrast gradient: black at the lower half, saturated blue at the upper half, fading into pale warm beige, with two precise circular arcs. Generate a 6x6 grid showing 36 unique variations of this product. Experiment wildly with color palettes, environments (studio, lifestyle, minimal, textured backgrounds), lighting styles, compositions, and moods. Keep product recognition and professional quality consistent, but make each cell visually distinct.

### No. 96: E-commerce Main Image - Figure Product Introduction Layout Prompt (Japanese)

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed, structured prompt for Nano Banana Pro (Japanese only) designed to transform a reference image character into a photorealistic 1/7 scale PVC figure product introduction layout. It includes placeholders for product name and manufacturer, and specifies complex layout elements like multiple close-up panels, inferred pricing, material, and size information, all presented with Japanese text.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
product_name: "{argument name="product name" default="ARBITRARY_PRODUCT_NAME"}"
manufacturer_name: "{argument name="manufacturer name" default="ARBITRARY_MANUFACTURER_NAME"}"

subject: >
  The character from reference image A, faithfully preserved in design, proportions,
  facial features, hairstyle, outfit details, and color palette.
  The character is transformed into a highly detailed, photorealistic PVC figure.
  Sculpting style and overall aesthetic are inferred directly from the reference image.
  The figure is presented as a 1/7 scale collectible.

composition: >
  Japanese-language product introduction layout inferred by the model.
  Vertical composition with a 3:4 aspect ratio.
  A large main visual of the full figure.
  A single, clearly defined product information area containing all textual elements.
  Product name logo and manufacturer name logo are each displayed exactly once.
  Multiple inset close-up panels are included.
  Each inset must focus on a different physical area or feature of the figure.
  No two inset panels may depict the same part or the same visual characteristic.
  Inset panels must be visually and conceptually distinct from one another.

action: >
  Static collectible figure pose with no movement.
  Emphasis on sculpt accuracy, proportions, and surface detail.

location: >
  Neutral studio-like environment inferred for product photography.
  Minimal, non-distracting background.

style: >
  Photorealistic product rendering and photography style.
  Artistic tone and mood inferred entirely from the reference image.

camera_lighting: >
  Camera angle and lighting inferred for clear presentation of a collectible figure.
  Realistic studio lighting interacting with PVC surfaces.
  Glossy highlights on hair and clothing.
  Matte finish on skin.
  Sharp focus with natural depth of field.
  Soft shadow beneath the figure as if placed on a flat surface.

colors: >
  Exact color reproduction based on the reference image.
  Background and graphic elements inferred to support readability of Japanese text.

text: >
  Product Name:
  ã€Œ{{product_name}}ã€
  â€» The product name must be displayed and shown as a logo only once.

  Manufacturer Name:
  ã€Œ{{manufacturer_name}}ã€
  â€» The manufacturer name must also be displayed and shown as a logo only once.

  Scale:
  1/7 Scale Figure

  Sculptor:
  {{manufacturer_name}}

  Price:
  The inferred retail price in Japanese Yen, based on the figure's scale, sculpting density, and paint expression.

  Size:
  The inferred overall height in centimeters, based on the character's body type and the 1/7 scale setting.

  Material:
  Appropriate material for a figure.
```

### No. 97: E-commerce Main Image - Surreal Product Shot Prompt: Purple Beverage Can with Organic Tendrils

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed JSON prompt for generating a surreal, advertisement-like product photo. It describes a purple beverage can suspended among glossy, organic, vine-like tendrils and roots, focusing on high contrast, specific lighting (studio key and rim lights), shallow depth of field, and micro-details like condensation.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "meta": {
    "image_quality": "High",
    "image_type": "Photo (styled/advertisement-like)"
  },

### No. 98: E-commerce Main Image - Museum-Quality Animal Portrait with Integrated Luxury Brand Pattern

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed, structured prompt for generating a museum-quality, ultra-detailed portrait of an animal (e.g., dog, fish, bird) on a pure white or black background. The core feature is the integration of a luxury brand's iconic pattern (like Louis Vuitton's monogram) into the animal's natural markings (spots, stripes, scales) in a clear and recognizable manner, maintaining an elegant, high-end commercial aesthetic.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
MUSEUM-QUALITY ultra-detailed {argument name="animal name" default="[animal name]"} portrait, pure {argument name="background color" default="white/black"} background, professional studio photography, 8K resolution. This must be BREATHTAKINGLY BEAUTIFUL and ELEGANT.

PERFECT POSE - FULL BODY VISIBLE (CRITICAL):
- The {argument name="animal name" default="[animal name]"} is captured in graceful side profile view, facing left
- {argument name="pose description" default="[pose description: Standing pose for dogs/cats | Swimming pose for fish | Sitting pose for birds | Flying pose for butterflies]"}
- The COMPLETE animal is visible from head to tail/fins/wings to all legs/paws/feet
- Elegant posture - {argument name="elegant posture" default="[back straight for mammals | body curved for fish | wings spread for birds]"}, displaying perfect {argument name="breed/species" default="[breed/species]"} proportions
- Head held with dignity and grace
- The animal appears poised, noble, and regal like a fine art subject
- Overall silhouette shows complete graceful body lines in their most beautiful form

COMPOSITION (CRITICAL):
- FULL BODY of the animal is visible within the frame
- The animal occupies the central 60-70% of the image
- Generous {argument name="background color" default="background color"} negative space around all sides (top, bottom, left, right)
- Animal is centered with balanced spacing
- Clean, minimalist, gallery-worthy composition
- High-end luxury brand campaign aesthetic

BASE COLOR/TEXTURE:
{argument name="base description based on animal" default="[base description based on animal]"}
For spotted animals (Dalmatian, Leopard, Koi fish): 
  - Pristine {argument name="base color" default="white/golden/orange"} base with natural {argument name="texture" default="texture: fur/scales/feathers"}
  - The base color is luminous and clean
  
For solid color animals (Black cat, White dove, Golden retriever):
  - {argument name="base color" default="[Base color]"} coat/fur/feathers with silky sheen
  - Natural highlights defining body structure

BRAND PATTERN INTEGRATION - {argument name="brand name" default="[brand name]"} (CLEAR AND RECOGNIZABLE):

PRIMARY (55-60% - Natural animal patterns):
- Natural {argument name="natural pattern" default="spots/stripes/scales/feathers"} in organic distribution
- Maintains the authentic look of the {argument name="animal species" default="[animal species]"}
- Irregular, asymmetric patterns true to nature

SECONDARY (40-45% - CLEAR Brand Elements):
The {argument name="natural pattern elements" default="natural pattern elements"} are strategically arranged and shaped to clearly form recognizable {argument name="brand name" default="[brand name]"} motifs:

Brand: {argument name="brand" default="[Louis Vuitton]"}
Core visual elements: {argument name="core visual elements" default="[LV monogram letters, quatrefoil four-petal flowers, geometric diamonds]"}

On the MAIN BODY (most visible area - torso/back/side):
- Multiple clear "{argument name="core logo" default="[core logo]"}" formed by connected {argument name="pattern connection" default="spots/stripes/markings"} - making them easily readable and recognizable
- Several {argument name="brand iconic pattern" default="[brand iconic pattern]"} clearly visible - {argument name="example" default="[example: quatrefoil flower shapes formed by 4 rounded spots in clover pattern]"}
- {argument name="decorative geometric pattern" default="[decorative geometric pattern]"} between the main logos

On the HEAD and NECK area:
- 1-2 smaller {argument name="logo" default="[Logo]"} formations  
- {argument name="iconic pattern" default="[iconic pattern]"} near the {argument name="facial features" default="ear/eye/facial features"}

On the LEGS/TAIL/WINGS/FINS:
- {argument name="geometric pattern or repeating motif" default="[geometric pattern or repeating motif]"} suggesting the brand's signature pattern

Pattern execution requirements:
- The {argument name="brand core elements" default="[brand core elements]"} should be CLEARLY RECOGNIZABLE at first glance - not abstract hints
- {argument name="pattern elements" default="[Pattern elements]"} are arranged in organized repeating pattern like {argument name="brand" default="[brand]"} signature print/canvas
```

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

{
  "subject": {
    "description": "Young woman in fitting room trying on ultra mini tennis skirt, wearing her own bikini top, mirror selfie",

    },

      "mouth": "soft pout, lips slightly parted"
    }
  },

  "clothing": {
    "top": {
      "item": "black triangle bikini top",

      "fit": "snug, enhancing chest"
    },
    "bottom": {
      "item": "white pleated tennis skirt",
      "style": "ultra mini, high waisted",
      "fit": "dangerously short, high on thigh",
      "detail": "retail price tag hanging visibly from waistband"
    },
    "feet": {
      "state": "bare feet",

    }
  },

    "type": "mirror selfie",
    "arm_action": {

    },

### No. 101: E-commerce Main Image - Two-Phase Prompt for Absurd Product Fusion Concepts

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A two-phase prompt for Nano Banana Pro designed to fuse everyday objects into new, absurd yet plausible inventions. Phase 1 analyzes the function, material, and cultural DNA of three reference objects. Phase 2 generates a 3x3 grid of photorealistic 3D concepts in a Dieter Rams/Dyson style, complete with minimalist labels.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
PHASE 1 PROMPT: Analyze these [{argument name="object 1" default="OBJECT 1"}], [{argument name="object 2" default="OBJECT 2"}], [{argument name="object 3" default="OBJECT 3"}] images. Extract: 1) Primary function, 2) Material DNA (metal/plastic ratio, texture), 3) Ergonomic signature (grip angle, weight distribution), 4) Mechanical principle, 5) Cultural association. Output as structured JSON.

PHASE 2 PROMPT: Create a 3x3 grid of photorealistic product renderings on a pristine white background. Each cell must be a hyper-realistic 3D concept that fuses elements from the previous analysis. For each invention, add minimalist navy blue text in Helvetica Neue: [Invention Name], [Core Mechanism], [Use Case]. Style: Dieter Rams meets Dyson - clean, technical, premium. Include subtle shadows and a 1px gold border on each cell. Make inventions absurd yet plausible (e.g., "Acoustic Peeler: uses sound waves to strip vegetables").
```

### No. 115: Game Asset - AKIRA 'Slide Brake Scene' Recreation Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly specific, multi-section prompt for Nano Banana Pro designed to recreate the iconic 'slide brake scene' from the anime AKIRA, without using the word 'AKIRA'. It details composition, subject, action, visual effects (smoke trails, neon-green energy arcs), and art style (1980s cyberpunk anime aesthetic).

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
(VARIABLE SCENE - EDIT HERE):
Nighttime, expansive {argument name="cityscape" default="Neo-Tokyo"} highway. Futuristic cityscape background with neon lights.
Strong one-point perspective: The road stretches straight from the bottom edge to the vanishing point in the center.

(CRITICAL COMPOSITION):
One-point perspective composition with the subject in the CENTER.
Subject Orientation: The motorcycle is shown in SIDE PROFILE (facing Screen Left).
TILT ANGLE: The motorcycle body is LEANING HEAVILY TOWARDS THE CAMERA (The top of the bike is closer to the viewer than the wheels).
Movement direction: The bike is sliding away from the camera, moving from the foreground deep into the background.
Placement: Bike is perfectly centered in the frame.

(SUBJECT):
A futuristic motorcycle and rider.
Motorcycle:
- Heavy, solid, rounded silhouette
- Minimal exposed mechanics, smooth cowling
- Wide, thick, high-grip tires
- Color scheme harmonized with rider
Rider:
- Face and outfit preserved from reference image
- Stare straight into the camera, glaring with a powerful, piercing gaze.
- Left foot planted firmly on the ground, struggling to support the heavy leaning bike
- Rider's leg is fully extended to brace against the fall

(ACTION & MECHANICS):
High-speed linear slide braking (NOT cornering).
The bike is sliding sideways while traveling backwards into the depth of the scene.
Instability: The bike is on the verge of falling over towards the screen.
Wheels are locked (not rotating).

(VISUAL EFFECTS - SMOKE TRAILS):
Three distinct, straight trails of thick white smoke.
Direction: Smoke stretches from the IMMEDIATE FOREGROUND (bottom of screen) directly to the motorcycle's wheels and rider's foot in the center.
The smoke trails act as leading lines pointing to the subject.
Violent debris and asphalt fragments kicking up.

(ENERGY EFFECTS):
Neon-green lightning energy arcs (1980s anime style) embedded within the white smoke trails.
Green energy flows through the smoke, following the straight lines from foreground to the bike.

(ART STYLE):
Cel-shaded animation, 1980s anime aesthetic (Cyberpunk).
High contrast, bold black shadows, dramatic lighting.
Poster-quality, ultra-high resolution, sharp focus.
```

### No. 118: Game Asset - Y2K Style Translucent Motorbike Product Design

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A prompt for generating a hyper-realistic, high-contrast product design image of a translucent dark motorbike with large wheels, featuring a biker in baggy camo and an oversized black hoodie. The style is inspired by Teenage Engineering and Y2K aesthetics, rendered using Octane with dynamic side view and fast shutter effect.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Translucent Dark motorbike with big wheels with a biker pilot bended on his motorbike full speed with large camo baggy and black oversized hoodie and short hair, wearing {argument name="glasses brand" default="Gentle Monster"} glasses, visible complex motor on the back, dynamic side view, product design minimalism, in the style of {argument name="design style 1" default="Teenage Engineering"} and {argument name="design style 2" default="Y2K style"}. matte plastic surfaces, plain gray background studio lighting, hyper-realistic. Octane render, cinematic framing fast shutter effect, high contrast, sharp bike details, professional motorsport photography style, 4K ultra realistic high-speed feeling, shallow depth of field.
```

### No. 120: Game Asset - Object-to-Dystopian Building Transformation

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A multi-step prompt instructing the AI to transform a small uploaded desktop object (like a stapler) into a monumental, dystopian Brutalist concrete building, generating blueprints, an eye-level street view, and an interior lobby shot.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Task: Turn small desktop objects into monumental dystopian buildings. 

Step 1: Upload image.... e.g. a {argument name="object" default="stapler"}

Step 2: Scale this object up by 5000%. It is now the headquarters for a villainous mega-corporation in a Brutalist concrete future. Analyze the geometry to create habitable floors."

Step 3 Output: 2x2 Grid.
Grid 1 & 2: Blueprints of the "Object turned into Tower" showing elevator shafts and executive suites.
Grid 3: Eye-level street view looking up at the concrete mega-structure in rain and fog. Tiny people for scale. Neon cyberpunk signs attached to the exterior.
Grid 4: Interior shot of the lobby, retaining the plastic curves of the original object but rendered in cold concrete and glass.
```

</div>

## ğŸ¤ How to Contribute

We welcome contributions! You can submit prompts via:

### ğŸ› GitHub Issue

1. Click [**Submit New Prompt**](https://github.com/YouMind-OpenLab/awesome-nano-banana-pro-prompts/issues/new?template=submit-prompt.yml)
2. Fill in the form with prompt details and image
3. Submit and wait for team review
4. If approved (we'll add `approved` label), it will automatically sync to CMS
5. Your prompt will appear in README within 4 hours

**Note:** We only accept submissions via GitHub Issues to ensure quality control.

See [CONTRIBUTING.md](docs/CONTRIBUTING.md) for detailed guidelines.
